## 3. Key Topics

- Organizational restructuring across Taliaz corporate and HealthyMind clinic, Leadership/role definitions and boundaries (COO
- CMO
- CMIO/Chief Medical Officer)
- including authority vs. responsibility alignment, Clinic governance model: reporting lines
- decision rights
- and oversight/steering committee concept, Resource allocation and shared services between corporate and clinic (operations
- HR
- finance
- budgets), Operational model discussions (pod-based team structure) and execution framework, 2026 planning and expansion considerations (structure to support scale), Conflict/mediation around ownership
- accountability
- and organizational design tradeoffs (notably Oren–Rami alignment issues)

שיש לך עכשיו, אם אתה רוצה כבר לזוז, לזוז, תעשה דברים שאתה, שבאים לך טוב.
